Oh my god, anyone who has done home decoration knows how difficult it is to ask workers to polish the edges of furniture so finely! The funniest thing is that my mother kept touching the table and praising the good quality. The old lady understands

I personally like thoughtful hotels. For example, if stationery, paper and pens are prepared, it is very good. This hotel actually has a special large stationery box for stationery, which hits my point~

Others, although the facilities are not particularly new, of course they are good to use, so the facilities are deducted 0.5

The location is convenient, you can walk to the Wuguang business district, go shopping in the nearby shopping malls and see the exhibition

服務：挺好的。接待都很耐心。

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Deluxe Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in May 2023
info:Friends
info:1 Review
rating:1
posted:Posted May 22, 2023
msg:説實話很不推薦這家酒店，本來預訂了兩晚，住了一晚趕緊退房換酒店了。
環境上，附近是個大工地，並不因為在K11附近周圍就繁華。
設施上，攜程上寫的2018年裝修，但客房設備老舊，説是2008年裝修我都相信。抽水馬桶半夜使用後上水十餘次，聲音巨大。
衞生上，我閨蜜睡了一晚之後腳上被咬了好幾個大包，不是蚊子咬的，懷疑是被褥或者地毯上的跳蚤叮咬所致。
服務上，電話前台要電蚊香，半小時後前台問我不好意思忘記你要啥了？告訴是要電蚊香又過了半小時才送來。門廊裏遇到打掃衞生的阿姨，我問能不能拿兩瓶水？人家説，最多兩瓶哈，不許多拿。
行吧，以上真的是最近幾年來最差的住店體驗，沒有之一，各位看官慎選這家。
